\usepackage[tightpage,active]{preview}
\newbox\lthtmlPageBox
\newdimen\lthtmlCropMarkHeight
\newdimen\lthtmlCropMarkDepth
\long\def\lthtmlTightVBox#1#2{%
    \setbox\lthtmlPageBox\vbox{\hbox{\catcode`\_=8 #2}}%
    \lthtmlCropMarkHeight=\ht\lthtmlPageBox \advance \lthtmlCropMarkHeight 6pt
    \lthtmlCropMarkDepth=\dp\lthtmlPageBox
    \lthtmltypeout{^^J:#1:lthtmlCropMarkHeight:=\the\lthtmlCropMarkHeight}%
    \lthtmltypeout{^^J:#1:lthtmlCropMarkDepth:=\the\lthtmlCropMarkDepth:1ex:=\the \dimexpr 1ex}%
    \begin{preview}\copy\lthtmlPageBox\end{preview}}}%
\long\def\lthtmlTightFBox#1#2{%
    \adjustnormalsize\setbox\lthtmlPageBox=\vbox\bgroup %
    \let\ifinner=\iffalse \let\)\liih@math %
    {\catcode`\_=8 #2}%
    \@next\next\@currlist{}{\def\next{\voidb@x}}%
    \expandafter\box\next\egroup %
    \lthtmlCropMarkHeight=\ht\lthtmlPageBox \advance \lthtmlCropMarkHeight 6pt
    \lthtmlCropMarkDepth=\dp\lthtmlPageBox
    \lthtmltypeout{^^J:#1:lthtmlCropMarkHeight:=\the\lthtmlCropMarkHeight}%
    \lthtmltypeout{^^J:#1:lthtmlCropMarkDepth:=\the\lthtmlCropMarkDepth:1ex:=\the \dimexpr 1ex}%
    \begin{preview}\copy\lthtmlPageBox\end{preview}}%
    \long\def\lthtmlinlinemathA#1#2\lthtmlindisplaymathZ{\lthtmlTightVBox{#1}{#2}}
    \def\lthtmlinlineA#1#2\lthtmlinlineZ{\lthtmlTightVBox{#1}{#2}}
    \long\def\lthtmldisplayA#1#2\lthtmldisplayZ{\lthtmlTightVBox{#1}{#2}}
    \long\def\lthtmlinlinemathA#1#2\lthtmlindisplaymathZ{\lthtmlTightVBox{#1}{#2}}
    \def\lthtmlinlineA#1#2\lthtmlinlineZ{\lthtmlTightVBox{#1}{#2}}
    \long\def\lthtmldisplayA#1#2\lthtmldisplayZ{\lthtmlTightVBox{#1}{#2}}
    \long\def\lthtmldisplayB#1#2\lthtmldisplayZ{\\edef\preveqno{(\theequation)}%
        \lthtmlTightVBox{#1}{\let\@eqnnum\relax#2}}
    \long\def\lthtmlfigureA#1#2\lthtmlfigureZ{\let\@savefreelist\@freelist
        \lthtmlTightFBox{#1}{#2}\global\let\@freelist\@savefreelist}
    \long\def\lthtmlpictureA#1#2\lthtmlpictureZ{\let\@savefreelist\@freelist
        \lthtmlTightVBox{#1}{#2}\global\let\@freelist\@savefreelist}
\def\lthtmlcheckvsize{\ifdim\ht\sizebox<\vsize 
  \ifdim\wd\sizebox<\hsize\expandafter\hfill\fi \expandafter\vfill
  \else\expandafter\vss\fi}%

{\bf p}_{{\bf v}_2}({\bf x})=\frac{{\bf v}_2^T{\bf x}}{{\bf v}_2^T{\bf v}_2}{\bf v}_2
=3\left[\begin{array}{c}0\\1\end{array}\right]
=\left[\begin{array}{c}0\\3\end{array}\right]$%
\lthtmlindisplaymathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\;\;\;\;\;\;\;\;\;

\lthtmlindisplaymathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_indisplay20594}%
$\displaystyle f_d({\bf\lambda}^*,{\bf\mu}^*)= L({\bf x}^*,{\bf\lambda}^*,{\bf\mu}^*)
=f_p({\bf x}^*)-{\bf\lambda}^{*T}{\bf h}({\bf x}^*)-{\bf\mu}^{*T}{\bf g}({\bf x}^*)$%
\lthtmlindisplaymathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_indisplay20598}%
$\displaystyle f_p({\bf x}^*)-{\bf\mu}^{*T}{\bf g}({\bf x}^*) =f_p({\bf x}^*)=p^*$%
\lthtmlindisplaymathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_indisplay20600}%
$\displaystyle \left\{\begin{array}{ll}
\bigtriangledown_{\bf x} L({\bf x}^*,{\bf\lambda},{\bf\mu})
=\bigtriangledown_{\bf x} f({\bf x}^*)
-\sum_{i=1}^m\lambda_i \bigtriangledown_{\bf x} h_i({\bf x}^*)
-\sum_{j=1}^n\mu_j     \bigtriangledown_{\bf x} g_j({\bf x}^*)={\bf0}
& \mbox{(stationarity)}  \\
\left\{\begin{array}{l}
h_i({\bf x}^*)=0,\;\;\;\;\;(i=1,\cdots,m)\\
g_j({\bf x}^*)\le 0\;\;\mbox{or}\;\; g_j({\bf x}^*)\ge 0,\;\;\;
(j=1,\cdots,n)
\end{array}\right.&\mbox{(primal feasibility)}  \\
\mu_j^*\le 0,\;\;\mbox{or}\;\;\mu_j^*\ge 0,\;\;\;\;(j=1,\cdots,n)&
\mbox{(dual feasibility)} \\
\mu_j^*\,g_j({\bf x}^*)=0,\;\;\;\;\;(j=1,\cdots,n) &
\mbox{(complementarity)}
\end{array}\right.$%
\lthtmlindisplaymathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_inline20612}%

\lthtmlindisplaymathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\lthtmlindisplaymathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

2x_1+ x_2 \le 18\\6x_1+5x_2 \le 60 \\2x_1+5x_2 \le 40 \\x_1 \ge 0,\;\; x_2\ge 0
\end{array}\right.
\end{array}
\;\;\;\;\;\;\mbox{or}\;\;\;\;\;\;
\begin{array}{ll}
\mbox{maximize}    & f_p({\bf x})={\bf c}^T{\bf x} \\
\mbox{subject to:} &
\left\{ \begin{array}{l}{\bf A}{\bf x}\le{\bf b}\\{\bf x}\ge {\bf0}
\end{array}\right.
\end{array}\end{displaymath}%
\lthtmldisplayZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

\left\{ \begin{array}{l}
2x_1+ x_2 \le 18\\6x_1+5x_2 \le 60 \\2x_1+5x_2 \le 40 \\
x_1 \ge 0,\;\; x_2\ge 0
\end{array}\right.
\end{array}
\;\;\;\;\;\;\Longrightarrow\;\;\;\;\;\;
\begin{array}{ll}
\mbox{maximize}    & f_p(x_1,x_2)=2x_1+3x_2 \\
\mbox{subject to:} &
\left\{ \begin{array}{l}
2x_1+ x_2+s_1=18\\6x_1+5x_2+s_2=60 \\2x_1+5x_2+s_3=40 \\
x_1 \ge 0,\; x_2\ge 0,\; s_1\ge 0,\; s_2\ge 0,\; s_3\ge0
\end{array}\right.
\end{array}\end{displaymath}%
\lthtmldisplayZ

\mbox{subject to:} &
\left\{ \begin{array}{l}
2x_1+ x_2+s_1=18\\6x_1+5x_2+s_2=60 \\2x_1+5x_2+s_3=40 \\
x_1 \ge 0,\; x_2\ge 0,\; s_1\ge 0,\; s_2\ge 0,\; s_3\ge0
\end{array}\right.
\end{array}\end{displaymath}%

{\bf g}({\bf x})\ge{\bf0}\\

\end{array}\right.\end{array}\end{displaymath}%
\lthtmldisplayZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage

{\bf g}({\bf x})\ge{\bf0}\;\Longrightarrow \;
{\bf g}({\bf x})-{\bf s}={\bf0}$%

\mbox{subject to:} &
\left\{\begin{array}{l}
{\bf h}({\bf x})={\bf0}\\

\end{array}\right.\end{array}\end{displaymath}%

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_indisplay21465}%
$\displaystyle L({\bf x},{\bf\lambda},{\bf\mu})=f({\bf x})
+{\bf\lambda}^T{\bf h}({\bf x})-{\bf\mu}^T{\bf x}$%
\lthtmlindisplaymathZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmldisplayA{displaymath21467}%
\begin{displaymath}\left\{
\begin{array}{ll}
\bigtriangledown_{\bf x} L({\bf x},{\bf\lambda},{\bf\mu})
={\bf g}_f({\bf x})+{\bf J}_{\bf h}^T({\bf x}){\bf\lambda}-{\bf\mu}
={\bf0}&
\mbox{(stationarity)}\\
{\bf h}({\bf x})={\bf0},\;\;\;\;{\bf x}\ge{\bf0} &
\mbox{(primal feasibility)}\\
{\bf\mu}\ge {\bf0} & \mbox{(dual feasibility)}\\
\mu_j x_j=0,\;\;\;\;(j=1,\cdots,N)\;\;\;\;\mbox{or}\;\;\;
{\bf XM1}={\bf0} & \mbox{(complementarity)}
\end{array}\right.\end{displaymath}%
\lthtmldisplayZ
\lthtmlcheckvsize\clearpage}

{\newpage\clearpage
\lthtmlinlinemathA{tex2html_wrap_indisplay21477}%
$\displaystyle {\bf X}=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}x_1&\cdots&0\\
\vdots&\ddots&\vdots\\0&\cdots&x_n \end{array}\right]_{N\times N},
\;\;\;\;\;
{\bf M}=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}\mu_1&\cdots&0\\
\vdots&\ddots&\vdots\\0&\cdots&\mu_N
\end{array}\right]_{N\times N},
\;\;\;\;\;
{\bf J}_{\bf h}({\bf x})=\left[\begin{array}{ccc}
\frac{\partial h_1}{\partial x_1}&\cdots&
\frac{\partial h_1}{\partial x_n}\\
\vdots & \ddots & \vdots\\
\frac{\partial h_m}{\partial x_1}&\cdots&
\frac{\partial h_m}{\partial x_n}\end{array}\right]_{M\times N}$%

\end{array}\right.
\end{array}

\begin{array}{ll}

\mbox{subject to:} &
\left\{ \begin{array}{l}
2x_1+x_2+x_3=18\\6x_1+5x_2+x_4=60 \\2x_1+5x_2+x_5=40 \\x_i \ge 0,\;\;(i=1,\cdots,5)
